   <div class="content">
    <article>
     <div class="post post-3336 type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-architecture tag-contemporary-architects tag-contemporary-homes tag-design-your-home tag-modern-home tag-modern-house" id="post-3336">
      <img alt="panorama house design with grass view from outside" class="attachment-thumbnail-single-image wp-post-image" height="450" src="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/panorama-house-design.jpg" width="600"/>
      <div class="entry-top">
       <h1 class="article-title entry-title">
        How to Design Your Homes Like Contemporary Architects
       </h1>
       <div class="article-author-img">
        <img alt="" class="avatar avatar-60 photo" height="60" src="http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/42d763be42ab2e002856c5309369e6fb?s=60&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g" srcset="http://1.gravatar.com/avatar/42d763be42ab2e002856c5309369e6fb?s=120&amp;d=mm&amp;r=g 2x" width="60"/>
       </div>
       <div class="views-nr">
        880
        <div class="clear">
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="article-meta">
       </div>
       <div class="article-meta vcard author">
        <span class="fn">
         by
         <a href="http://www.faburous.com/author/sunshine-xieanzee/" rel="author" title="Posts by Sunshine Xieanzee">
          Sunshine Xieanzee
         </a>
        </span>
       </div>
       <div class="article-meta updated">
        9 months  ago
       </div>
       <div class="article-meta">
        In
        <a href="http://www.faburous.com/category/architecture/" rel="category tag">
         Architecture
        </a>
       </div>
       <div class="clear">
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="clear">
      </div>
      <div class="entry">
       <!-- entry content -->
       <!-- Easy Plugin for AdSense V8.60 -->
       <!-- [leadin: 0 urCount: 0 urMax: 0] -->
       <div class="ezAdsense adsense adsense-leadin" style="float:left;margin:12px;">
        <script async="" src="//pagead2.googlesyndication.com/pagead/js/adsbygoogle.js">
        </script>
        <!-- Faburous Under Post Title -->
        <ins class="adsbygoogle" data-ad-client="ca-pub-1144763503132051" data-ad-slot="5479052785" style="display:inline-block;width:336px;height:280px">
        </ins>
        <script>
         (adsbygoogle = window.adsbygoogle || []).push({});
        </script>
       </div>
       <!-- Easy Plugin for AdSense V8.60 -->
       <p>
        Contemporary architects surround us every day and its influence to us is undeniable. Our dwellings, workplaces, school and churches are examples of these. With the fast-growing technology, the societys buildings are also expected to be in harmony with technological advancement. A lot of people nowadays are defying the traditional architecture and prefers the elements of contemporary ones. Many of us are in awe when we see the beauty of these contemporary architectures. If you are planning to construct your dream house, weve gathered interesting ideas on how you can design your new home.
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         Modern Living Room With Panoramic Ocean View
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
        <a class="wp-img-bg-off" href="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/modern-living-room-with-Panoramic-ocean-view.jpeg" rel="mygallery">
         <img alt="You can design your house with open windows or glass windows" class="alignnone wp-image-10337" height="480" src="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/modern-living-room-with-Panoramic-ocean-view-700x466.jpeg" width="721"/>
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        If you are lucky to have chosen a location that offers a visually appealing view, then take advantage of it. You can design your house with open windows or glass windows. Panoramic views just like the images above are definitely a plus point when constructing a house. They are not only good for the eyes, but they also provide us with relaxation, and strong immersive feelings. Its like standing on top of the world without leaving the comfort of your homes.
       </p>
       <p>
        <img alt="metal kitchen " class="alignnone wp-image-10403" height="572" src="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/Aluminum-and-Stainless-Steel-Kitchen.jpg" width="764"/>
       </p>
       <p>
        Many of the contemporary designs are made of steel and metal just like commercial and industrial buildings. But now, many homes are also made from these materials. Obviously, this is a very good choice since these materials are durable. They are safe to use because they cant be destroyed by pests. Moreover, a lot of builders choose the aforementioned materials because they are flexible, stable and reliable. This means that your homes will be standing for a relatively long period of time. Notice in the images above, how fine-looking the kitchens are when you use stainless steel materials.
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         Panorama House Design
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
        <a class="wp-img-bg-off" href="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/panorama-house-design.jpg" rel="mygallery">
         <img alt="panorama house design with grass view from outside" class="alignnone wp-image-10332" height="533" src="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/panorama-house-design.jpg" width="711"/>
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        This Panorama view is not only good for the eyes, but also provide us with relaxation, and strong immersive feelings. Its like standing on top of the world without leaving the comfort of your homes. This house design looks good with grass view from outside.
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         Modern Kitchen With Stainless Steel Counter
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
        <a class="wp-img-bg-off" href="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/Modern-kitchen-with-stainless-steel-counter.jpg" rel="mygallery">
         <img alt="Stainless steel is safe to use because it cant be destroyed by pests" class="alignnone wp-image-10336" height="473" src="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/Modern-kitchen-with-stainless-steel-counter.jpg" width="710"/>
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        This is a modern kitchen with stainless steel counter. Many of the contemporary designs are made of steel and metal just like commercial and industrial buildings. But now, many homes are also made from these materials. Obviously, this is a very good choice since these materials are durable. They are safe to use because they cant be destroyed by pests.
       </p>
       <p>
        If you are looking for beautiful contemporary house designs with high ceilings, the images above would be of great help. Most of contemporary house designs advocate high ceilings, flexible floor space and
        <a class="autobesttag" href="http://www.faburous.com/topics/minimal/" rel="nofollow" title="See the tag: minimal (3 posts)">
         minimal
        </a>
        decorations. The usual size of ceilings before was 8-foot tall, but now many home builders consider 9-foot ceiling as the standard. With high ceilings you can allow natural light to penetrate into your homes and for obvious reason, they are more spacious. Likewise, with tall ceilings, you can hung paintings, add and modern furniture.
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         Modern Monochromatic Living Room
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
        <a class="wp-img-bg-off" href="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/Modern-Monochromatic-Living-Room.jpg" rel="mygallery">
         <img alt="Modern monochromatic livingroom with wood wall panel and dark furniture" class="alignnone wp-image-10338" height="538" src="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/Modern-Monochromatic-Living-Room-700x529.jpg" width="712"/>
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        Many contemporary architects continually support innovative and creative home designs. For instance, many of them appreciate the minimalist interiors for they offer neat and simple yet elegant appearance as shown on the two images above.The simplicity of these designs seems to relieve us from daily stresses just by looking at how beautiful these interiors are.
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         Modern African Graphic Colour Monochromatic
         <a class="autobesttag" href="http://www.faburous.com/topics/interior/" rel="nofollow" title="See the tag: interior (2 posts)">
          Interior
         </a>
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
        <a class="wp-img-bg-off" href="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/modern-african-graphic-colour-monochromatic-interior.jpg" rel="mygallery">
         <img alt="The walls and floor paints are of monochromatic colors" class="alignnone size-full wp-image-10335" height="474" src="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/modern-african-graphic-colour-monochromatic-interior.jpg" width="700"/>
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        This image illustrates a geometric design with the living rooms rectangular shape proportionate to the overall space of the house. Likewise, it is also seen that in the picture, the
        <a class="autobesttag" href="http://www.faburous.com/topics/walls/" rel="nofollow" title="See the tag: walls (2 posts)">
         walls
        </a>
        and floor paints are of monochromatic colors. The combination of different shades of gray, black and brown colors create a smooth and balanced look. With the appropriate textures your house will still appear vibrant even if you are using monochromatic colors.
       </p>
       <p>
        <strong>
         Amazing Modern Home Design
        </strong>
       </p>
       <p>
        <a class="wp-img-bg-off" href="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/breathtaking-image-of-amazing-modern-home-design.jpg" rel="mygallery">
         <img alt="breathtaking image of amazing modern home design" class="alignnone wp-image-10334" height="621" src="http://www.faburous.com/wp-content/uploads/2014/10/breathtaking-image-of-amazing-modern-home-design.jpg" width="704"/>
        </a>
       </p>
       <p>
        Remember it is of great pride that we have a structure we can call home. The picture above shows a striking contemporary house design. Whatever design you choose for your house, make sure it suits your needs as well as the needs of your family. It is always a good feeling to go home to a beautifully constructed contemporary house.
       </p>
       <!--www.crestaproject.com Cresta Social Share Counter Content Start-->

        <div class="sbutton-total" id="total-shares-content">

       <br/>
       <p>
        Sunshine graduated with a Degree of BSIED Drafting Technology. She once dreamed of running her own online business firm and first began writing and designing websites from a young age. She developed a passion for  Houses, building and Interior designing  and began taking on clients while still in college.

Sunshine oversees the creative direction at Sunshine Outsourcing as well as business development. Sunshine's charm and willingness to talk to anyone and everyone has been key to building our large local client base.
 
Sunshine is very generous and a true leader to her firm and people
